Imagine walking into a casino and you see Kevin Hart sitting in front of a slot machine. He's emaciated and chained to the handle. The only words he can wisp out are, "do... you love slots? ... I do.." He feverishly keeps playing. Every time he wins, he lets out a feverish and bloodcurdling wail that would invoke the envy of the wildest of banshees. You don't know how to handle this. So, you walk away. He grabs your arm and stares into your soul with dead eyes, gaining energy from your shared gaze. His eyes bulge and his lips curl. He gasps, then whispers, "win... big..". Then suddenly, his mouth expands to the size of a dinner plate, protruding outward and inhaling voraciously. Bodies all around the slot machines start falling like dominoes. You look at their screens and notice that they had all just lost. Kevin Hart looks at you dead in the eyes and says, "I am now full. I can now leave." And then, he vanishes in a cloud of sulfur, gold dust and terrible jokes. The ritual is complete and now you are chained to the wretched machine in place of the last washed up comedian.
